{BaudhDhS, 1, 4}

ātmani eva asya caturthaḥ pādaḥ pariśiṣyate | [BaudhDhS, 1, 4 511697_2]

{BaudhDhS, 1, 6}
atha kamaṇḍalucaryām upadiśanti | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 1.1]
chāgasya dakṣiṇe karṇe pāṇau viprasya dakṣiṇe | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 2.1]
apsu caiva kuśastambe pāvakaḥ paripaṭhyate | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 2.2]
tasmācchaucaṃ kṛtvā pāṇinā parimṛjīta paryagnikaraṇaṃ hi tat uddīpyasva jātaveda iti punardāhād viśiṣyate | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 3.1]
tatrāpi kiṃcit saṃspṛṣṭaṃ manasi manyeta kuśairvā tṛṇair vā prajvālya pradakṣiṇaṃ paridahanam | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 4.1]
ata ūrdhvaṃ śvavāyasaprabhṛtyupahatānām agnivarṇa ityupadiśanti | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 4.2]
mūtrapurīṣalohitaretaḥprabhṛtyupahatānām utsargaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 5.1]
bhagne kamaṇḍalau vyāhṛtibhiḥ śataṃ juhuyāj japed vā | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 6.1]
bhūmir bhūmim agān mātā mātaram apyagāt bhūyāsma putraiḥ paśubhir yo no dveṣṭi sa bhidyatām iti | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 7.1]
kapālāni saṃhṛtyāpsu prakṣipya sāvitrīṃ daśāvarāṃ kṛtvā punar evānyaṃ gṛhṇīyāt | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 7.2]
varuṇam āśritya etat te varuṇa punar eva mām om iti akṣaraṃ dhyāyet | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 8.1]
śūdrād gṛhya śataṃ kuryād vaiśyād ardhaśataṃ smṛtam | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 9.1]
kṣatriyāt pañcaviṃśat tu brāhmaṇād daśa kīrtitāḥ | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 9.2]
astamita āditya udakaṃ gṛhṇīyān na gṛhṇīyād iti mīmāṃsante brahmavādinaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 10.1]
gṛhṇīyād ity etad aparam | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 11.1]
yāvad udakaṃ gṛhṇīyāt tāvat prāṇam āyacchet | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 12.1]
agnir ha vai hy udakaṃ gṛhṇāti | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 13.1]
kamaṇḍalūdakenābhiṣiktapāṇipādo yāvad ārdraṃ tāvadaśuciḥ pareṣām ātmānam eva pūtam karoti nānyat karma kurvīteti vijñāyate | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 14.1]
api vā pratiśaucam ā maṇibandhācchucir iti baudhāyanaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 15.1]
athāpy udāharanti | [BaudhDhS, 1, 6 16.1]
{BaudhDhS, 1, 7}
kamaṇḍalur dvijātīnāṃ śaucārthaṃ vihitaḥ purā | [BaudhDhS, 1, 7 1.1]
brahmaṇā munimukhyaiś ca tasmāt taṃ dhārayet sadā | [BaudhDhS, 1, 7 1.2]
tataḥ śaucaṃ tataḥ pānaṃ saṃdhyopāsanam eva ca | [BaudhDhS, 1, 7 2.1]
nirviśaṅkena kartavyaṃ yadīcchecchreya ātmanaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 1, 7 2.2]
kuryācchuddhena manasā na cittaṃ dūṣayed budhaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 1, 7 3.1]
saha kamaṇḍalunotpannaḥ svayaṃbhūs tasmāt kamaṇḍalunā caret | [BaudhDhS, 1, 7 3.2]

{BaudhDhS, 2, 8}

āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhiḥ | [BaudhDhS, 2, 8 13.2]

pavamānaḥ suvarjana iti | [BaudhDhS, 2, 8 13.4]
etenānuvākena mārjayitvāntarjalagato 'ghamarṣaṇena trīn prāṇāyāmān dhārayitvottīrya vāsaḥ pīḍayitvā prakṣālitopavātāny akliṣṭāni vāsāṃsi paridhāyāpa ācamya darbheṣv āsīno darbhān dhārayamāṇaḥ prāṅmukhaḥ sāvitrīṃ sahasrakṛtva āvartayecchatakṛtvo 'parimitakṛtvo vā daśāvaram | [BaudhDhS, 2, 8 13.5]

{BaudhDhS, 2, 17}

avāritasthāneṣu pathiṣu vā kṣetreṣu vāpratihatāvakāśeṣu vā yatra yatrauṣadhayo vidyante tatra tatraikaikaṃ kaṇiśam uñchayitvā kāle kāle śilair vartayatīti śiloñchā | [BaudhDhS, 3, 2 14.2]
kāpoteti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 2 15.1]
avāritasthāneṣu pathiṣu vā kṣetreṣu vāpratihatāvakāśeṣu vā yatra yatrauṣadhayo vidyante tatra tatrāṅgulībhyām ekaikām oṣadhim uñchayitvā saṃdaṃśanāt kapotavad iti kāpotā | [BaudhDhS, 3, 2 15.2]
siddheccheti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 2 16.1]
vṛttibhiḥ śrānto vṛddhatvād dhātukṣayād vā sajjanebhyaḥ siddham annam icchatīti siddhecchā | [BaudhDhS, 3, 2 16.2]
tasyātmani samāropaṇaṃ vidyate saṃnyāsivad upacāraḥ pavitrakāṣāyavāsovarjam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 2 17.1]
vānyāpi vṛkṣalatāvallyoṣadhīnāṃ ca tṛṇauṣadhīnāṃ ca śyāmākajartilādīnām | [BaudhDhS, 3, 2 18.1]
vanyābhir vartayatīti vānyā | [BaudhDhS, 3, 2 18.2]
athāpy udāharanti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 2 19.1]
mṛgaiḥ saha parispandaḥ saṃvāsas tebhir eva ca | [BaudhDhS, 3, 2 19.2]
tair eva sadṛśī vṛttiḥ pratyakṣaṃ svargalakṣaṇam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 2 19.3]
pratyakṣaṃ svargalakṣaṇam iti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 2 20.1]
{BaudhDhS, 3, 3}
atha vānaprasthadvaividhyam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 1.1]
pacamānakā apacamānakāś ceti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 2.1]
tatra pacamānakāḥ pañcavidhāḥ sarvāraṇyakā vaituṣikāḥ kandamūlabhakṣāḥ phalabhakṣāḥ śākabhakṣāś ceti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 3.1]
tatra sarvāraṇyakā nāma dvividhā dvividham āraṇyam āśrayanta indrāvasiktā retovasiktāś ceti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 4.1]
tatrendrāvasiktā nāma vallīgulmalatāvṛkṣāṇām ānayitvā śrapayitvā sāyamprātaragnihotraṃ hutvā yatyatithivratibhyaś ca dattvāthetaraccheṣabhakṣāḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 5.1]
retovasiktā nāma māṃsaṃ vyāghravṛkaśyenādibhir anyatamena vā hatam ānayitvā śrapayitvā sāyamprātaragnihotraṃ hutvā yatyatithivratibhyaś ca dattvāthetaraccheṣabhakṣāḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 6.1]
vaituṣikās tuṣadhānyavarjaṃ taṇḍulān ānayitvā śrapayitvā sāyamprātaragnihotraṃ hutvā yatyatithivratibhyaś ca dattvāthetaraccheṣabhakṣāḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 7.1]
kandamūlaphalaśākabhakṣāṇām apy evam eva | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 8.1]
pañcaivāpacamānakā unmajjakāḥ pravṛttāśino mukhenādāyinas toyāhārā vāyubhakṣāś ceti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 9.1]
tatronmajjakā nāma lohāśmakaraṇavarjam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 10.1]
hastenādāya pravṛttāśinaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 11.1]
mukhenādāyino mukhenādadate | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 12.1]
toyāhārāḥ kevalaṃ toyāhārāḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 13.1]
vāyubhakṣā nirāhārāś ca | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 14.1]
iti vaikhānasānāṃ vihitā daśa dīkṣāḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 15.1]
yaḥ svaśāstram abhyupetya daṇḍaṃ ca maunaṃ cāpramādaṃ ca | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 16.1]
vaikhānasāḥ śudhyanti nirāhārāś ceti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 17.1]
śāstraparigrahaḥ sarveṣāṃ brahmavaikhānasānām | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 18.1]
na druhyed daṃśamaśakān himavāṃs tāpaso bhavet | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 19.1]
vanapratiṣṭhaḥ saṃtuṣṭaś cīracarmajalapriyaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 19.2]
atithīn pūjayet pūrvaṃ kāle tv āśramam āgatān | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 20.1]
devaviprāgnihotre ca yuktas tapasi tāpasaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 20.2]
kṛcchrāṃ vṛttim asaṃhāryāṃ sāmānyāṃ mṛgapakṣibhiḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 21.1]
tadaharjanasaṃbhārāṃ kaṣāyakaṭukāśrayām | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 21.2]
parigṛhya śubhāṃ vṛttim etāṃ durjanavarjitām | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 22.1]
vanavāsam upāśritya brāhmaṇo nāvasīdati | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 22.2]
mṛgaiḥ saha parispandaḥ saṃvāsas tebhir eva ca | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 23.1]
tair eva sadṛśī vṛttiḥ pratyakṣaṃ svargalakṣaṇam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 23.2]
pratyakṣaṃ svargalakṣaṇam iti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 3 24.1]
{BaudhDhS, 3, 4}
atha yadi brahmacāry avratyam iva caren māṃsaṃ vāśnīyāt striyaṃ vopeyāt sarvāsv evārtiṣu | [BaudhDhS, 3, 4 1.1]
antarāgāre 'gnim upasamādhāya saṃparistīryāgnimukhāt kṛtvāthājyāhutīr upajuhoti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 4 2.1]
kāmena kṛtaṃ kāmaḥ karoti kāmāyaivedaṃ sarvaṃ yo mā kārayati tasmai svāhā | [BaudhDhS, 3, 4 2.2]
manasā kṛtaṃ manaḥ karoti manasa evedaṃ sarvaṃ yo mā kārayati tasmai svāhā | [BaudhDhS, 3, 4 2.3]
rajasā kṛtaṃ rajaḥ karoti rajasa evedaṃ sarvaṃ yo mā kārayati tasmai svāhā | [BaudhDhS, 3, 4 2.4]
tamasā kṛtaṃ tamaḥ karoti tamasa evedaṃ sarvaṃ yo mā kārayati tasmai svāhā | [BaudhDhS, 3, 4 2.5]
pāpmanā kṛtaṃ pāpmā karoti pāpmana evedaṃ sarvaṃ yo mā kārayati tasmai svāhā | [BaudhDhS, 3, 4 2.6]
manyunā kṛtaṃ manyuḥ karoti manyava evedaṃ sarvaṃ yo mā kārayati tasmai svāheti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 4 2.7]
jayaprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt | [BaudhDhS, 3, 4 3.1]
apareṇāgniṃ kṛṣṇājinena prācīnagrīveṇottaralomnā prāvṛtya vasati | [BaudhDhS, 3, 4 4.1]
vyuṣṭāyāṃ jaghanārdhād ātmānam apakṛṣya tīrthaṃ gatvā prasiddhaṃ snātvāntarjalagato 'ghamarṣaṇena ṣoḍaśa prāṇāyāmān dhārayitvā prasiddham ādityopasthānāt kṛtvācāryasyagṛhān eti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 4 5.1]
yathāśvamedhāvabhṛtha evam evaitad vijānīyād iti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 4 6.1]
{BaudhDhS, 3, 5}
athātaḥ pavitrātipavitrasyāghamarṣaṇasya kalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 5 1]
tīrthaṃ gatvā snātaḥ śucivāsā udakānte sthaṇḍilam uddhṛtya sakṛtklinnena vāsasā sakṛtpūrṇena pāṇinādityābhimukho 'ghamarṣaṇaṃ svādhyāyam adhīyīta | [BaudhDhS, 3, 5 2]
prātaḥ śataṃ madhyāhne śatam aparāhṇe śatam aparimitaṃ vā | [BaudhDhS, 3, 5 3]
uditeṣu nakṣatreṣu prasṛtiyāvakaṃ prāśnīyāt | [BaudhDhS, 3, 5 4]
jñānakṛtebhyo 'jñānakṛtebhyaś copapātakebhyaḥ saptarātrāt pramucyate dvādaśarātrād bhrūṇahananaṃ gurutalpagamanaṃ suvarṇastainyaṃ surāpānam iti ca varjayitvā | [BaudhDhS, 3, 5 5]
ekaviṃśatirātrāt tāny api tarati tāny api jayati | [BaudhDhS, 3, 5 6]
sarvaṃ tarati sarvaṃ jayati sarvakratuphalam avāpnoti sarveṣu tīrtheṣu snāto bhavati sarveṣu vedeṣu cīrṇavrato bhavati sarvair devair jñāto bhavaty ā cakṣuṣaḥ paṅktiṃ punāti karmāṇi cāsya sidhyantīti baudhāyanaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 5 7]
{BaudhDhS, 3, 6}
atha karmabhir ātmakṛtair gurum ivātmānaṃ manyetātmārthe prasṛtiyāvakaṃ śrapayed uditeṣu nakṣatreṣu | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 1.1]
na tato 'gnau juhuyāt | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 2.1]
na cātra balikarma | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 3.1]
aśṛtaṃ śrapyamāṇaṃ śṛtaṃ cābhimantrayeta | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 4.1]
yavo 'si dhānyarājo 'si vāruṇo madhusaṃyutaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 5.1]
nirṇodaḥ sarvapāpānāṃ pavitram ṛṣibhiḥ smṛtam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 5.2]
ghṛtaṃ yavā madhu yavā āpo vā amṛtaṃ yavāḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 5.3]
sarvaṃ punīta me pāpaṃ yan mayā duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 5.4]
vācā kṛtaṃ karma kṛtaṃ manasā durvicintitam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 5.5]
alakṣmīṃ kālakarṇīṃ ca sarvaṃ punīta me yavāḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 5.6]
śvasūkarāvadhūtaṃ ca kākocchiṣṭahataṃ ca yat | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 5.7]
mātāpitror aśuśrūṣāṃ sarvaṃ punīta me yavāḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 5.8]
mahāpātakasaṃyuktaṃ dāruṇaṃ rājakilbiṣam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 5.9]
bālavṛddham adharmaṃ ca sarvaṃ punīta me yavāḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 5.10]
suvarṇastainyam avratyam ayājyasya ca yājanam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 5.11]
brāhmaṇānāṃ parīvādaṃ sarvaṃ punīta me yavāḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 5.12]
gaṇānnaṃ gaṇikānnaṃ ca śūdrānnaṃ śrāddhasūtakam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 5.13]
corasyānnaṃ navaśrāddhaṃ sarvaṃ punīta me yavā iti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 5.14]
śrapyamāṇe rakṣāṃ kuryāt | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 6.1]
namo rudrāya bhūtādhipataye | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 6.2]
dyauḥ śāntā | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 6.3]
kṛṇuṣva pājaḥ prasitiṃ na pṛthvīm ity etenānuvākena | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 6.4]
ye devāḥ puraḥsado 'gninetrā rakṣohaṇa iti pañcabhiḥ paryāyaiḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 6.5]
mā nas toke | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 6.6]
brahmā devānām iti dvābhyām | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 6.7]
śṛtaṃ ca laghv aśnīyāt prayataḥ pātre niṣicya | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 7.1]
ye devā manojātā manoyujaḥ sudakṣā dakṣapitāras te naḥ pāntu te no 'vantu tebhyo namas tebhyaḥ svāheti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 8.1]
ātmani juhuyāt | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 8.2]
trirātraṃ medhārthī | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 9.1]
ṣaḍrātraṃ pītvā pāpakṛcchuddho bhavati | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 10.1]
saptarātraṃ pītvā bhrūṇahananaṃ gurutalpagamanaṃ suvarṇastainyaṃ surāpānam iti ca punāti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 11.1]
ekādaśarātraṃ pītvā pūrvapuruṣakṛtam api pāpaṃ nirṇudati | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 12.1]
api vā goniṣkrāntānāṃ yavānām ekaviṃśatirātraṃ pītvā gaṇān paśyati gaṇādhipatiṃ paśyati vidyāṃ paśyati vidyādhipatiṃ paśyatīty āha bhagavān baudhāyanaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 6 13.1]
{BaudhDhS, 3, 7}
kūśmāṇḍair juhuyād yo 'pūta iva manyeta | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 1.1]
yathā steno yathā bhrūṇahaivam eṣa bhavati yo 'yonau retaḥ siñcati | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 2.1]
yad arvācīnam eno bhrūṇahatyāyās tasmān mucyata iti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 3.1]
ayonau retaḥ siktvānyatra svapnād arepā vā pavitrakāmaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 4.1]
amāvāsyāyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vā keśaśmaśrulomanakhāni vāpayitvā brahmacārikalpena vratam upaiti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 5.1]
saṃvatsaraṃ māsaṃ caturviṃśatyahaṃ dvādaśa rātrīḥ ṣaṭ tisro vā | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 6.1]
na māṃsam aśnīyān na striyam upeyān noparyāsīta jugupsetānṛtāt | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 7.1]

tadvidheṣu yavāgūṃ rājanyo vaiśya āmikṣām | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 9.1]
pūrvāhṇe pākayajñikadharmeṇāgnim upasamādhāya saṃparistīryāgnimukhāt kṛtvāthājyāhutīr upajuhoti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 10.1]
yad devā devaheḍanam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 10.2]

āyuṣ ṭe viśvato dadhad iti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 10.4]
etais tribhir anuvākaiḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 10.5]
pratyṛcam ājyasya juhuyāt | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 11.1]
siṃhe vyāghra uta yā pṛdākāv iti catasraḥ sruvāhutīḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 12.1]
agne 'bhyāvartin | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 12.2]
agne aṅgiraḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 12.3]
punar ūrjā | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 12.4]

yan mayā manasā vācā kṛtam enaḥ kadācana | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 13.1]

athāgnyādheye | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 16.1]

pūrṇāhutīḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 7 16.5]

{BaudhDhS, 3, 8}
athātaś cāndrāyaṇasya kalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 1.1]
śuklacaturdaśīm upavaset | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 2.1]
keśaśmaśrulomanakhāni vāpayitvāpi vā śmaśrūṇy evāhataṃ vāso vasānaḥ satyaṃ bruvann āvasatham abhyupeyāt | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 3.1]
tasminn asya sakṛtpraṇīto 'gnir araṇyor nirmanthyo vā | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 4.1]
brahmacārī suhṛt praiṣāyopakalpī syāt | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 5.1]
haviṣyaṃ ca vratopāyanīyam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 6.1]
agnim upasamādhāya saṃparistīryāgnimukhāt kṛtvā pakvāj juhoti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 7.1]
agnaye yā tithiḥ syān nakṣatrāya sadaivatāya | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 8.1]
atrāha gor amanvateti cāndramasīṃ pañcamīṃ dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ ṣaṣṭhīm ahorātrābhyāṃ saptamīṃ raudrīm aṣṭamīṃ saurīṃ navamīṃ vāruṇīṃ daśamīm aindrīmekādaśīṃ vaiśvadevīṃ dvādaśīm iti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 8.2]
athāparāḥ samāmananti digbhyaś ca sadaivatābhya uror antarikṣāya sadaivatāya | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 9.1]
navo navo bhavati jāyamāna iti sauviṣṭakṛtīṃ hutvāthaitaddhavirucchiṣṭaṃ kaṃse vā camase vā vyuddhṛtya haviṣyair vyañjanair upasicya pañcadaśa piṇḍān prakṛtisthān prāśnāti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 10.1]
prāṇāya tveti prathamam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 11.1]
apānāya tveti dvitīyam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 11.2]
vyānāya tveti tṛtīyam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 11.3]
udānāya tveti caturtham | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 11.4]
samānāya tveti pañcamam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 11.5]
yadā catvāro dvābhyāṃ pūrvam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 11.6]
yadā trayo dvābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ pūrvau | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 11.7]
yadā dvau dvābhyāṃ pūrvaṃ tribhir uttaram | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 11.8]
ekaṃ sarvaiḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 11.9]
nigrābhyā stheti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 12.1]
apaḥ pītvāthājyāhutīr upajuhoti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 12.2]
prāṇāpānavyānodānasamānā me śudhyantāṃ jyotir ahaṃ virajā vipāpmā bhūyāsaṃ svāhā | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 12.3]
vāṅmanaḥ śiraḥpāṇi tvakcarmamāṃsaṃ pṛthivyaptejo annamayaprāṇamayamanomayavijñānamayānandamayā me śudhyantāṃ jyotir ahaṃ virajā vipāpmā bhūyāsaṃ svāheti saptabhir anuvākaiḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 12.4]
jayaprabhṛti siddham ā dhenuvarapradānāt | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 13.1]

tvam agne vratapā asīti prabuddhaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 16.1]

amedhyaṃ dṛṣṭvā japati | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 18.1]
abaddhaṃ mano daridraṃ cakṣuḥ sūryo jyotiṣāṃ śreṣṭho dīkṣe mā mā hāsīr iti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 18.2]
prathamāyām aparapakṣasya caturdaśa grāsān | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 19.1]
evam ekāpacayenāmāvāsyāyāḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 20.1]
amāvāsyāyāṃ grāso na vidyate | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 21.1]
atha prathamāyāṃ pūrvapakṣasyaikaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 22.1]
dvau dvitīyāyām | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 22.2]
evam ekopacayenā paurṇamāsyāḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 23.1]
paurṇamāsyāṃ sthālīpākasya juhoty agnaye yā tithiḥ syān nakṣatrebhyaś ca sadaivatebhyaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 24.1]
purastācchroṇāyā abhijitaḥ sadaivatasya hutvā gāṃ brāhmaṇebhyo dadyāt | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 25.1]
tad etac cāndrāyaṇaṃ pipīlikāmadhyam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 26.1]
viparītaṃ yavamadhyam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 8 26.2]

{BaudhDhS, 3, 9}

haviṣyam annam icched apaḥ phalāni vā | [BaudhDhS, 3, 9 3.1]
grāmāt prācīṃ vodīcīṃ vā diśam upaniṣkramya gomayena gocarmamātraṃ caturaśraṃ sthaṇḍilam upalipya prokṣya lakṣaṇam ullikhya adbhir abhyukṣya agnim upasamādhāya saṃparistīryaitābhyo devatābhyo juhuyāt | [BaudhDhS, 3, 9 4.1]

apratibhāyāṃ yāvatā kālena na veda tāvantaṃ kālaṃ tad adhīyīta sa yadā jānīyād ṛkto yajuṣṭaḥ sāmata iti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 9 8.1]

dvādaśa vedasaṃhitā adhīyīta | [BaudhDhS, 3, 9 10.1]
yad anenānadhyāye 'dhīyīta yad guravaḥ kopitā yāny akāryāṇi bhavanti tābhiḥ punīte | [BaudhDhS, 3, 9 10.2]
śuddham asya pūtaṃ brahma bhavati | [BaudhDhS, 3, 9 10.3]
ata ūrdhvaṃ saṃcayaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 9 11.1]
aparā dvādaśa vedasaṃhitā adhītya tābhir uśanaso lokam avāpnoti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 9 12.1]

anaśnan saṃhitāsahasram adhīyīta | [BaudhDhS, 3, 9 15.1]
brahmabhūto virajo brahma bhavati | [BaudhDhS, 3, 9 15.2]
saṃvatsaraṃ bhaikṣaṃ prayuñjāno divyaṃ cakṣur labhate | [BaudhDhS, 3, 9 16.1]
ṣaṇ māsān yāvakabhakṣaś caturo māsān udakasaktubhakṣo dvau māsau phalabhakṣo māsam abbhakṣo dvādaśarātraṃ vāprāśnan kṣipram antardhīyate jñātīn punāti saptāvarān sapta pūrvān ātmānaṃ pañcadaśaṃ paṅktiṃ ca punāti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 9 17.1]
tām etāṃ devaniśrayaṇīty ācakṣate | [BaudhDhS, 3, 9 18.1]
etayā vai devā devatvam agacchann ṛṣaya ṛṣitvam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 9 19.1]

brāhmaṇebhyaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 9 21.2]
{BaudhDhS, 3, 10}
ukto varṇadharmaś cāśramadharmaś ca | [BaudhDhS, 3, 10 1.1]
atha khalv ayaṃ puruṣo yāpyena karmaṇā mithyā vā caraty ayājyaṃ vā yājayaty apratigrāhyasya vā pratigṛhṇāty anāśyānnasya vānnam aśnāty acaraṇīyena vā carati | [BaudhDhS, 3, 10 2.1]

kuryād ity eva | [BaudhDhS, 3, 10 5.1]

sarvaṃ pāpmānaṃ tarati tarati brahmahatyāṃ yo 'śvamedhena yajata iti | [BaudhDhS, 3, 10 7.2]
agniṣṭutā vābhiśasyamāno yajeteti ca | [BaudhDhS, 3, 10 8.1]
tasya niṣkrayaṇāni japas tapo homa upavāso dānam | [BaudhDhS, 3, 10 9.1]
upaniṣado vedādayo vedāntāḥ sarvacchandaḥsu saṃhitā madhūny aghamarṣaṇam atharvaśiro rudrāḥ puruṣasūktaṃ rājanarauhiṇe sāmanī bṛhadrathaṃtare puruṣagatir mahānāmnyo mahāvairājaṃ mahādivākīrtyaṃ jyeṣṭhasāmnām anyatamaṃ bahiṣpavamānaḥ kūśmāṇḍyaḥ pāvamānyaḥ sāvitrī ceti pāvanāni | [BaudhDhS, 3, 10 10.1]
upasannyāyena payovratatā śākabhakṣatā phalabhakṣatā mūlabhakṣatā prasṛtiyāvako hiraṇyaprāśanaṃ ghṛtaprāśanaṃ somapānam iti medhyāni | [BaudhDhS, 3, 10 11.1]
sarve śiloccayāḥ sarvāḥ sravantyaḥ saritaḥ puṇyā hradās tīrthāny ṛṣiniketanāni goṣṭhakṣetrapariṣkandā iti deśāḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 10 12.1]
ahiṃsā satyam astainyaṃ savaneṣūdakopasparśanaṃ guruśuśrūṣā brahmacaryam adhaḥśayanam ekavastratānāśaka iti tapāṃsi | [BaudhDhS, 3, 10 13.1]
hiraṇyaṃ gaur vāso 'śvo bhūmis tilā ghṛtam annam iti deyāni | [BaudhDhS, 3, 10 14.1]
saṃvatsaraḥ ṣaṇmāsāś catvāras trayo dvāv ekaś caturviṃśatyaho dvādaśāhaḥ ṣaḍahas tryaho 'horātra ekāha iti kālāḥ | [BaudhDhS, 3, 10 15.1]
etāny anādeśe kriyeran | [BaudhDhS, 3, 10 16.1]
enaḥsu guruṣu gurūṇi laghuṣu laghūni | [BaudhDhS, 3, 10 17.1]

{BaudhDhS, 4, 1}

{BaudhDhS, 4, 2}

teṣu teṣu ca doṣeṣu garīyāṃsi laghūni ca | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 1.2]

abhojyānāṃ tu sarveṣām abhojyānnasya bhojane | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 5.1]
ṛgbhis taratsamandībhir mārjanaṃ pāpaśodhanam | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 5.2]

vidhinā yena mucyante pātakebhyo 'pi sarvaśaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 6.2]
prāṇāyāmān pavitrāṇi vyāhṛtīḥ praṇavaṃ tathā | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 7.1]

trirātraṃ vāyubhakṣo vā klinnavāsāḥ plutaḥ śuciḥ | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 8.1]
pratiṣiddhāṃs tathācārān abhyasyāpi punaḥpunaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 9.1]
vāruṇībhir upasthāya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyata iti | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 9.2]
athāvakīrṇy amāvāsyāyāṃ niśy agnim upasamādhāya dārvihomikīṃ pariceṣṭāṃ kṛtvā dve ājyāhutī juhoti | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 10.1]
kāmāvakīrṇo 'smy avakīrṇo 'smi kāma kāmāya svāhā | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 10.2]

hutvā prayatāñjaliḥ kavātiryaṅṅ agnim upatiṣṭheta | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 11.1]
saṃ mā siñcantu marutaḥ sam indraḥ saṃ bṛhaspatiḥ | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 11.2]
saṃ māyam agniḥ siñcatv āyuṣā ca balena cāyuṣmantaṃ karotu meti | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 11.3]
prati hāsmai marutaḥ prāṇān dadhati pratīndro balaṃ prati bṛhaspatir brahmavarcasaṃ praty agnir itarat sarvam | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 11.4]
sarvatanur bhūtvā sarvam āyur eti | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 11.5]
trir abhimantrayeta | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 11.6]
triṣatyā hi devā iti vijñāyate | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 11.7]
yo 'pūta iva manyeta ātmānam upapātakaiḥ | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 12.1]
sa hutvaitena vidhinā sarvasmāt pāpāt pramucyate | [BaudhDhS, 4, 2 12.2]

sūnavo yasya śiṣyā vā juhvaty aṣṭau gaṇān imān | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 9.1]
adhyāpanaparikrītair aṃhasaḥ so 'pi mucyate | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 9.2]
dhanenāpi parikrītair ātmapāpajighāṃsayā | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 10.1]
hāvanīyā hy aśaktena nāvasādyaḥ śarīradhṛk | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 10.2]
dhanasya kriyate tyāgaḥ karmaṇāṃ sukṛtām api | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 11.1]
puṃso 'nṛṇasya pāpasya vimokṣaḥ kriyate kvacit | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 11.2]
vimukto vidhinaitena sarvapāpārṇasāgarāt | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 12.1]
ātmānaṃ manyate śuddhaṃ samarthaṃ karmasādhane | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 12.2]
sarvapāpārṇamuktātmā kriyā ārabhate tu yāḥ | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 13.1]
ayatnenaiva tāḥ siddhiṃ yānti śuddhaśarīriṇaḥ | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 13.2]
prājāpatyam idaṃ puṇyam ṛṣiṇā samudīritam | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 14.1]
idam adhyāpayen nityaṃ dhārayecchṛṇute 'pi vā | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 14.2]
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo brahmaloke mahīyate | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 14.3]
yān siṣādhayiṣur mantrān dvādaśāhāni tāñ japet | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 15.1]
ghṛtena payasā dadhnā prāśya niśy odanaṃ sakṛt | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 15.2]
daśavāraṃ tathā homaḥ sarpiṣā savanatrayam | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 16.1]
pūrvasevā bhaved eṣāṃ mantrāṇāṃ karmasādhane | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 16.2]
mantrāṇāṃ karmasādhana iti | [BaudhDhS, 4, 8 16.3]
